#Unrest 0: Politically Controversial TV Program (Left Unrest)
country_event = {
	id = mdmosjap_japan.100101
	title = mdmosjap_japan.100101.t
	desc = mdmosjap_japan.100101.d
	#picture = GFX_news_event_hearts_of_iron_4

	trigger = {
		original_tag = JAP
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 9600
		modifier = {
			trigger_mdmosjap_has_radicalism_left_0 = yes
			factor = 2
		}
		modifier = {
			trigger_mdmosjap_has_radicalism_left_1 = yes
			factor = 1
		}
		modifier = {
			trigger_mdmosjap_has_radicalism_left_10 = yes
			factor = 0.75
		}
		modifier = {
			trigger_mdmosjap_has_radicalism_left_25 = yes
			factor = 0.5
		}
		modifier = {
			trigger_mdmosjap_has_radicalism_left_50 = yes
			factor = 1
		}
	}

	#Defend Protester
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.100101.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.100101.oA"
		add_political_power = -10
		increase_mdmosjap_concon_left_1 = yes
		set_temp_variable = { jap_radical_change = 2 }
		jap_modify_radicalism_right = yes
	}

	#Neutral
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 80
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.100101.oB
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.100101.oB"
		set_temp_variable = { jap_radical_change = 1 }
		jap_modify_radicalism_left = yes
		set_temp_variable = { jap_radical_change = 1 }
		jap_modify_radicalism_right = yes
	}

	#Attack Protester
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.100101.oC
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.100101.oC"
		add_political_power = -10
		increase_mdmosjap_concon_right_1 = yes
		set_temp_variable = { jap_radical_change = 2 }

			factor = 80
		}

		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.101101.oB"

		set_temp_variable = { jap_radical_change = 2 }

#Unrest 50: An Invitation from the Leftist Meeting (Left Unrest)
country_event = {
	id = mdmosjap_japan.102101
	title = mdmosjap_japan.102101.t
	desc = mdmosjap_japan.102101.d
	#picture = GFX_news_event_hearts_of_iron_4

	trigger = {
		original_tag = JAP
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 28800
		modifier = {
			trigger_mdmosjap_has_radicalism_left_0 = yes
			factor = 100
		}
		modifier = {
			trigger_mdmosjap_has_radicalism_left_1 = yes
			factor = 1
		}
		modifier = {
			trigger_mdmosjap_has_radicalism_left_10 = yes
			factor = 1
		}
		modifier = {
			trigger_mdmosjap_has_radicalism_left_25 = yes
			factor = 1
		}
		modifier = {
			trigger_mdmosjap_has_radicalism_left_50 = yes
			factor = 0.05
		}
		modifier = {
			trigger_mdmosjap_has_radicalism_left_75 = yes
			factor = 2
		}
		modifier = {
			has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_NATIONAL_WORRYING
			factor = 2
		}
		modifier = {
			JAP = {
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_STATE_OF_EMERGENCY_SENTENCED
					has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_STATE_OF_EMERGENCY_INVOKED
				}
			}
			factor = 32
		}
	}

	#We don't need any sensitive supports like these radicalist.
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 98
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.102101.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.102101.oA"
		increase_mdmosjap_concon_left_2 = yes
		add_political_power = -100
	}

	#Thanks, I Hate it.
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
				factor = 0.01
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.102101.oB
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.102101.oB"
		set_temp_variable = { jap_radical_change = 2 }
		jap_modify_radicalism_left = yes
		set_temp_variable = { jap_radical_change = 1 }
		jap_modify_radicalism_right = yes
	}

	#They would be cultivated as a good supporters.
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
				factor = 0.01
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.102101.oC
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.102101.oC"
		increase_mdmosjap_concon_left_3 = yes
		set_temp_variable = { jap_radical_change = 1 }
		jap_modify_radicalism_left = yes
		set_temp_variable = { jap_radical_change = 2 }
		jap_modify_radicalism_right = yes
	}
}

#Unrest 50: An Invitation from the Rightist Meeting (Right Unrest)
country_event = {
	id = mdmosjap_japan.102151
	title = mdmosjap_japan.102151.t
	desc = mdmosjap_japan.102151.d
	#picture = GFX_news_event_hearts_of_iron_4

	trigger = {
		original_tag = JAP
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 28800
		modifier = {
			trigger_mdmosjap_has_radicalism_right_0 = yes
			factor = 100
		}
		modifier = {
			trigger_mdmosjap_has_radicalism_right_1 = yes
			factor = 1
		}
		modifier = {
			trigger_mdmosjap_has_radicalism_right_10 = yes
			factor = 1
		}
		modifier = {
			trigger_mdmosjap_has_radicalism_right_25 = yes
			factor = 1
		}
		modifier = {
			trigger_mdmosjap_has_radicalism_right_50 = yes
			factor = 0.05
		}
		modifier = {
			trigger_mdmosjap_has_radicalism_right_75 = yes
			factor = 2
		}
		modifier = {
			has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_JAP_APOLITICAL_FRIENDSHIP
			factor = 0.8
		}
		modifier = {
			JAP = {
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_STATE_OF_EMERGENCY_SENTENCED
					has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_STATE_OF_EMERGENCY_INVOKED
				}
			}
			factor = 32
		}
	}

	#We must not do any move.
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 98
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.102101.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.102151.oA"
		increase_mdmosjap_concon_right_2 = yes
		add_political_power = -100
	}

	#Make a public atmosphere to shut that streaming down.
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
				factor = 0.01
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.102101.oB
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.102151.oB"
		set_temp_variable = { jap_radical_change = 1 }
		jap_modify_radicalism_left = yes
		set_temp_variable = { jap_radical_change = 2 }
		jap_modify_radicalism_right = yes
	}

	#They would be sponsored by the government in secret.
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
				factor = 0.01
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.102101.oC
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.102101.oC"

		jap_modify_radicalism_left = yes
		set_temp_variable = { jap_radical_change = 1 }
		jap_modify_radicalism_right = yes
	}

#Unrest 75: Government's Blame against Mass Media (Leftist Government)
country_event = {
	id = mdmosjap_japan.103101
	title = mdmosjap_japan.103101.t
	desc = mdmosjap_japan.103101.d
	#picture = GFX_news_event_hearts_of_iron_4

	trigger = {
		original_tag = JAP
		OR = {
			is_in_array = { ruling_party = 2 }
			is_in_array = { ruling_party = 3 }
			is_in_array = { ruling_party = 4 }
			is_in_array = { ruling_party = 5 }
			is_in_array = { ruling_party = 17 }
			is_in_array = { ruling_party = 18 }
			is_in_array = { ruling_party = 19 }
		}
		NOT = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_STATE_OF_EMERGENCY_INVOKED }
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 21600
		modifier = {
			trigger_mdmosjap_has_radicalism_left_0 = yes
			factor = 1000
		}
		modifier = {
			trigger_mdmosjap_has_radicalism_left_1 = yes
			factor = 1
		}
		modifier = {
			trigger_mdmosjap_has_radicalism_left_10 = yes
			factor = 1
		}
		modifier = {
			trigger_mdmosjap_has_radicalism_left_25 = yes
			factor = 1
		}
		modifier = {
			trigger_mdmosjap_has_radicalism_left_50 = yes
			factor = 1
		}
		modifier = {
			trigger_mdmosjap_has_radicalism_left_75 = yes
			factor = 0.01
		}
		modifier = {
			trigger_mdmosjap_has_radicalism_left_90 = yes
			factor = 0.8
		}
		modifier = {
			has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_NATIONAL_WORRYING
			factor = 0.75
		}
		modifier = {
			has_stability < 0.50
			factor = 20
		}
		modifier = {
			JAP = {
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_STATE_OF_EMERGENCY_SENTENCED
					has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_STATE_OF_EMERGENCY_INVOKED
				}
			}
			factor = 32
		}
	}

	#Government is right
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.103101.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.103101.oA"
		increase_mdmosjap_concon_left_2 = yes
		increase_mdmosjap_concon_right_1 = yes
		set_temp_variable = { jap_radical_change = -2 }
		jap_modify_radicalism_left = yes
		set_temp_variable = { jap_radical_change = 1 }
		jap_modify_radicalism_right = yes
		add_stability = -0.01
	}

	#We must close our mouths now
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				OR = {
					NOT = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 4 } }
					NOT = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 5 } }
					NOT = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 6 } }
					NOT = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 7 } }
					NOT = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 15 } }
					NOT = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 20 } }
					NOT = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 21 } }
					NOT = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 22 } }
					NOT = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 23 } }
				}
				factor = 0.5
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.103101.oB
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.103101.oB"
		increase_mdmosjap_concon_left_1 = yes
		increase_mdmosjap_concon_right_1 = yes
		add_stability = -0.02
	}

	#The statement was wrong
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				OR = {
					NOT = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 4 } }

country_event = {
	id = mdmosjap_japan.130129001
	title = mdmosjap_japan.130129001.t
	desc = mdmosjap_japan.130129001.d
	#picture = GFX_news_event_hearts_of_iron_4

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	#Do not pressure them
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
			modifier = {
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				is_in_array = { ruling_party = 0 }
				is_in_array = { ruling_party = 1 }
				is_in_array = { ruling_party = 7 }
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.130129001.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.130129001.oA"
		add_popularity = { ideology = communism popularity = -0.01 }
		add_popularity = { ideology = nationalist popularity = 0.05 }
		add_political_power = -100
	}

	#Accuse dietmembers
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
		}
		trigger = {
			AND = {
				NOT = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 0 } }
				NOT = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 1 } }
				NOT = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 7 } }
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.130129001.oB
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.130129001.oB"
		add_popularity = { ideology = communism popularity = -0.03 }
		add_popularity = { ideology = nationalist popularity = -0.03 }
		mdmosjap_decrease_party_popularity_array_7_var_5 = yes
		set_temp_variable = { jap_radical_change = 2 }
		jap_modify_radicalism_right = yes
	}

	#You understand what we said, or you're gonna pay for this! Think Wisely!
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				OR = {
					has_country_leader = { name = "Koichi Kato" }
					has_country_leader = { name = "Yohei Kono" }
				}
				factor = 0.5
			}
			modifier = {
				OR = {
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 2 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 3 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 4 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 5 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 17 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 18 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 19 }
				}
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.130129001.oC
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.130129001.oC"
		add_popularity = { ideology = communism popularity = 0.01 }
		add_popularity = { ideology = nationalist popularity = 0.01 }
		increase_mdmosjap_concon_right_2 = yes
	}
}

#Battle of Amamioshima: Japan's Action
country_event = {
	id = mdmosjap_japan.131222002
	title = mdmosjap_japan.131222002.t
	desc = mdmosjap_japan.131222002.d
	#picture = GFX_news_event_hearts_of_iron_4

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		JAP = { set_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_BATTLE_OF_AMAMIOSHIMA }
	}

	#Ask China
	option = {
		ai_chance = { factor = 90 }
		name = mdmosjap_japan.131222002.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.131222002.oA"
		increase_mdmosjap_concon_right_2 = yes
		set_temp_variable = { jap_radical_change = 1 }
		jap_modify_radicalism_left = yes
		set_temp_variable = { jap_radical_change = 1 }
		jap_modify_radicalism_right = yes
		CHI = { country_event = mdmosjap_japan.131222003 }
	}

	#Keep Calm
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 5
			modifier = {
				is_in_array = { ruling_party = 3 }
				factor = 10
			}
			modifier = {
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.131222002.oB
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.131222002.oB"
		increase_mdmosjap_concon_left_2 = yes
		set_temp_variable = { jap_radical_change = 4 }
		jap_modify_radicalism_right = yes
		#add_national_unity = -0.05
		#add_popularity = { ideology = communism popularity = 0.05 }
		mdmosjap_decrease_ruling_party_popularity_5 = yes
		NKO = {
			add_opinion_modifier = { target = JAP modifier = recent_actions_positive }
		}
	}

	#Violate EEZ
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 5
			modifier = {
				has_government = nationalist
				factor = 10
			}
			modifier = {
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.131222002.oC
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.131222002.oC"
		increase_mdmosjap_concon_right_2 = yes
		set_temp_variable = { jap_radical_change = 4 }
		jap_modify_radicalism_left = yes
		add_popularity = { ideology = nationalist popularity = 0.05 }
		add_named_threat = { threat = 0.2 name = MDMOSJAP_JAP_PRCeez_violation_after_amamioshima }
		CHI = { country_event = mdmosjap_japan.131222006 }
		TAI = { country_event = mdmosjap_japan.131222007 }
	}
}

country_event = {

	title = mdmosjap_japan.151116001.t
	desc = mdmosjap_japan.151116001.d
	#picture = GFX_news_event_hearts_of_iron_4

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		JAP = {
			NOT = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 3 } }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_SDP_DOI_RESIGNED }
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		set_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_SDP_DOI_RESIGNED
	}

	option = {
		name = mdmosjap_japan.generic_interesting
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.151116001.generic_interesting"
		mdmosjap_decrease_party_popularity_array_3_var_1 = yes
		set_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_WESTSOC_MIZUHO_FUKUSHIMA
		increase_mdmosjap_concon_right_1 = yes
		set_temp_variable = { jap_radical_change = -1 }
		jap_modify_radicalism_left = yes
	}
}

#Dissolve of NCP(CP)
country_event = {
	id = mdmosjap_japan.151121001
	title = mdmosjap_japan.151121001.t
	desc = mdmosjap_japan.151121001.d
	#picture = GFX_news_event_hearts_of_iron_4

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = mdmosjap_japan.generic_interesting
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.151121001.generic_interesting"
		set_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_NCP_DISSOLUTION

		#LDP(Pro-US) + NCP(CP)
		set_temp_variable = { mdmosjap_temp_var_ldp_ncp_amalgamation_ncp_pop = party_pop_array^6 }
		set_temp_variable = { mdmosjap_temp_var_ldp_ncp_amalgamation_ncp_pop_minus = party_pop_array^6 }
		multiply_temp_variable = { mdmosjap_temp_var_ldp_ncp_amalgamation_ncp_pop_minus = -1 }
		set_variable = { party_pop_array^6 = 0.000 }
		add_popularity = { ideology = communism popularity = mdmosjap_temp_var_ldp_ncp_amalgamation_ncp_pop_minus }
		add_popularity = { ideology = democratic popularity = mdmosjap_temp_var_ldp_ncp_amalgamation_ncp_pop }
		add_to_variable = { party_pop_array^0 = mdmosjap_temp_var_ldp_ncp_amalgamation_ncp_pop }
		custom_effect_tooltip = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_NCP_DISSOLUTION_CALC_TT
		hidden_effect = { recalculate_party = yes update_government_coalition_strength = yes update_party_name = yes set_coalition_drift = yes }

		if = {
			limit = { is_in_array = { gov_coalition_array = 6 } }
			remove_from_array = { gov_coalition_array = 6 }
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 0 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 1 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 7 }
				}
			}
			increase_mdmosjap_concon_right_1 = yes		#Fortify LDP's Anti-Constitutional Theory
			set_temp_variable = { jap_radical_change = 1 }
			jap_modify_radicalism_right = yes
		} else = {
			increase_mdmosjap_concon_left_1 = yes
			set_temp_variable = { jap_radical_change = -1 }
			jap_modify_radicalism_right = yes
		}
	}
}

#Takeshima Day (Repeat Trigger)
country_event = {
	id = mdmosjap_japan.170316001
	title = mdmosjap_japan.170316001.t
	desc = mdmosjap_japan.170316001.d
	#picture = GFX_news_event_hearts_of_iron_4

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			country_exists = KOR
			country_exists = NKO
		}
	}

	#It's local government's decision
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 70
			modifier = {
				has_country_leader = { name = "Yohei Kono" }
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.170316001.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.170316001.oA"
		increase_mdmosjap_concon_right_2 = yes
		set_temp_variable = { jap_radical_change = 2 }
		jap_modify_radicalism_left = yes
		set_temp_variable = { jap_radical_change = 3 }
		jap_modify_radicalism_right = yes
		mdmosjap_increase_party_popularity_array_6_var_1 = yes
		mdmosjap_increase_party_popularity_array_7_var_1 = yes
		mdmosjap_increase_party_popularity_array_14_var_1 = yes
		mdmosjap_increase_party_popularity_array_20_var_1 = yes
		mdmosjap_increase_party_popularity_array_21_var_1 = yes
		mdmosjap_increase_party_popularity_array_22_var_1 = yes
		effect_tooltip = {
			KOR = { add_opinion_modifier = { target = JAP modifier = mdmosjap_opinion_PRK_takeshima_day } }
			NKO = { add_opinion_modifier = { target = JAP modifier = mdmosjap_opinion_PRK_takeshima_day } }
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			JAP = { country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.170316002 days = 365 } }
			KOR = { country_event = mdmosjap_japan.170316006 }
			NKO = { country_event = mdmosjap_japan.170316006 }
		#	news_event = mdmosjap_japannews.170316001
		}
		set_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_ALLOW_TAKESHIMA_DAY
	}

	#Interrupt local autonomy
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30
			modifier = {
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
				factor = 0
			}
			modifier = {
				OR = {
					has_government = nationalist
				}
				factor = 0.1	#Means factor = 3
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.170316001.oB
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.170316001.oB"
		increase_mdmosjap_concon_left_10 = yes
		set_temp_variable = { jap_radical_change = 5 }
		jap_modify_radicalism_right = yes
		mdmosjap_decrease_party_popularity_array_6_var_1 = yes
		mdmosjap_decrease_party_popularity_array_7_var_1 = yes
		mdmosjap_decrease_party_popularity_array_14_var_1 = yes
		mdmosjap_decrease_party_popularity_array_20_var_1 = yes
		mdmosjap_decrease_party_popularity_array_21_var_1 = yes
		mdmosjap_decrease_party_popularity_array_22_var_1 = yes
		effect_tooltip = {
			KOR = { add_opinion_modifier = { target = JAP modifier = recent_actions_positive } }
			NKO = { add_opinion_modifier = { target = JAP modifier = recent_actions_positive } }
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			JAP = { country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.170316002 days = 365 } }
			KOR = { country_event = mdmosjap_japan.170316007 }
			NKO = { country_event = mdmosjap_japan.170316007 }
		}
		set_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_DENY_TAKESHIMA_DAY
	}
}

#[HIDDEN] Takeshima Day Check
country_event = {
	id = mdmosjap_japan.170316002
	hidden = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	#Annual Ceremony of Takeshima Day
	option = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.170316002.oA"
		trigger = {
			JAP = {
				AND = {
					NOT = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_BAN_TAKESHIMA_DAY }
					NOT = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_END_TAKESHIMA_DAY }
				}
			}
		}
		JAP = { country_event = mdmosjap_japan.170316003 }
	}

	#End of Takeshima Day
	option = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.170316002.oB"
		trigger = {
			JAP = {
				AND = {
					NOT = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_BAN_TAKESHIMA_DAY }
					has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_END_TAKESHIMA_DAY
				}
			}
		}
		JAP = { country_event = mdmosjap_japan.170316004 }
	}

	#Takeshima Day Banned
	option = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.170316002.oC"
		trigger = {
			JAP = {
				AND = {
					has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_BAN_TAKESHIMA_DAY
					NOT = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_END_TAKESHIMA_DAY }
				}
			}
		}
		JAP = { country_event = mdmosjap_japan.170316005 }
	}
}

#Zaitokukai
#TODO: add choices for this or just move to news
country_event = {
	id = mdmosjap_japan.181203001
	title = mdmosjap_japan.181203001.t
	desc = mdmosjap_japan.181203001.d
	#picture = GFX_news_event_hearts_of_iron_4

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_government = nationalist }
	}

	option = {
		name = mdmosjap_japan.181203001.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.181203001.oA"
		mdmosjap_increase_party_popularity_array_20_var_5 = yes
		#create_country_leader = { name = "Makoto Sakurai" ideology = fascist_ideology picture = "Portrait_JAP_Makoto_Sakurai.dds" }
		add_stability = -0.01
		increase_mdmosjap_concon_right_1 = yes
		set_temp_variable = { jap_radical_change = 2 }
		jap_modify_radicalism_right = yes
		set_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_ZAITOKUKAI
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						NOT = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_LDP_COLLAPSE }
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 1 }
					}
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 0 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 6 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 7 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 15 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 20 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 21 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 22 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 23 }
				}
				NOT = { has_country_leader = { name = "Yasuo Fukuda" } }
				NOT = { has_country_leader = { name = "Yoshihide Suga" } }
				NOT = { has_country_leader = { name = "Fumio Kishida" } }
				NOT = { has_country_leader = { name = "Yohei Kono" } }
				NOT = { has_country_leader = { name = "Hiromu Nonaka" } }
			}
			add_country_leader_trait = uyoku_supporter
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 2 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 3 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 4 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 5 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 14 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 17 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 18 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 19 }
				}
			}
			add_country_leader_trait = sayoku_supporter
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_LDP_COLLAPSE
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 1 }
					}
					has_country_leader = { name = "Yasuo Fukuda" }
					has_country_leader = { name = "Yoshihide Suga" }
					has_country_leader = { name = "Fumio Kishida" }
					has_country_leader = { name = "Yohei Kono" }
					has_country_leader = { name = "Hiromu Nonaka" }
				}
			}
			add_country_leader_trait = conservative_lib
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = medium_far_right_movement }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = medium_far_right_movement
				add_idea = large_far_right_movement
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_idea = medium_far_right_movement } }
			add_ideas = medium_far_right_movement
		}
	}
}

#Kenkiho Recession
country_event = {
	id = mdmosjap_japan.190621001
	title = mdmosjap_japan.190621001.t
	desc = mdmosjap_japan.190621001.d
	#picture = GFX_news_event_hearts_of_iron_4

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = { set_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENTEXECUTED_KENKIHO_RECESSION }

	option = {
		name = mdmosjap_japan.190621001.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.190621001.oA"
		set_temp_variable = { jap_radical_change = 1 }
		jap_modify_radicalism_left = yes
		set_temp_variable = { jap_radical_change = 1 }
		jap_modify_radicalism_right = yes
		add_timed_idea = { idea = JAP_kenkiho_recession days = 730 }
		if = { limit = { has_idea = depression } add_stability = -0.03 }
		if = { limit = { has_idea = recession } swap_ideas = { remove_idea = recession add_idea = depression } }
		if = { limit = { has_idea = stagnation } swap_ideas = { remove_idea = stagnation add_idea = recession } }
		if = { limit = { has_idea = stable_growth } swap_ideas = { remove_idea = stable_growth add_idea = stagnation } }
		if = { limit = { has_idea = fast_growth } swap_ideas = { remove_idea = fast_growth add_idea = stable_growth } }
		if = { limit = { has_idea = economic_boom } swap_ideas = { remove_idea = economic_boom add_idea = fast_growth } }

		set_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_KENKIHO_RECESSION
	}
}

	is_triggered_only = yes

		add_stability = -0.05
		#TODO: bonus to liberals popularity
		set_temp_variable = { jap_radical_change = 15 }
		jap_modify_radicalism_left = yes
		set_temp_variable = { jap_radical_change = 10 }
		jap_modify_radicalism_right = yes
		#TODO: custom tooltip: will require us to spend money to escape the recession
		country_event = { id = Japan.100015020 days = 5 } #american financial crisis: hands across the pacific
	}

	#This is the fault of reckless globalization!
	option = {
		name = Japan.100015000.oB
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Japan.100015000.oB"
		decrease_two_level_economic_growth = yes
		remove_ideas = JAP_ftaap_member
		USA = {
			remove_ideas = JAP_ftaap_member
		}
		#TODO: big penalty to liberals popularity
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = JAP_ftaap_member
			}
			country_event = { id = Japan.100015010 random_days = 5 } #american financial crisis: dissolution of the FTAAP
		}
		country_event = { id = Japan.100015010 days = 7 } #american financial crisis: the shattering
	}
}

#American Financial Crisis: The Shattering
country_event = {
	id = Japan.100015010
	title = Japan.100015010.t
	desc = Japan.100015010.d
	desc = {
		text = Japan.100015010.d.a #USA left the FTAAP on bad terms
		trigger = {
			USA = {
				has_country_flag = JAP_RECESSION_USA_REJECTED_SOVEREIGNTY
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = Japan.100015010.d.b #JAP terminated the FTAAP in response to recession aftershocks
	}
	picture = WIP #TODO: gfx

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	#Free Trade with Asians Only
	option = {
		name = Japan.100015010.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Japan.100015010.oA"
		#TODO: EAEC invitation focuses should take less time to finish, higher penalty to include australia/nz
		add_ideas = JAP_seap_member
		if = {
			limit = {
				USA = {
					has_country_flag = JAP_RECESSION_USA_REJECTED_SOVEREIGNTY
				}
			}
			every_other_country = { #FTAAP exists but is collapsing with USA's exit
				limit = {
					has_idea = JAP_ftaap_member
				}
				country_event = { id = Japan.100015011 random_days = 2 random_hours = 12 } #american financial crisis: revive FTAAP as SEAP
			}
		}
		else = {
			every_other_country = { #invite countries that used to be in FTAAP and still want to be back
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = JAP_FTAAP_FORMER_MEMBER
				}
				country_event = { id = Japan.100015011 random_days = 2 random_hours = 12 } #american financial crisis: revive FTAAP as SEAP
			}
		}
	}

	#End Free Trade entirely!
	option = {
		name = Japan.100015010.oB
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Japan.100015010.oB"
		#TODO: EPA focuses should take less time to finish
		#TODO: big bonus to nationalist
	}
}

#American Financial Crisis: The American-Japanese Market (JAP/USA)
country_event = {
	id = Japan.100015025
	title = Japan.100015025.t
	desc = Japan.100015025.d
	picture = WIP #TODO: gfx

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	#A Toast To Trans-Pacific Hegemony!
	option = {
		name = Japan.100015025.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Japan.100015025.oA"
		if = {
			limit = {
				original_tag = JAP
			}
			add_ideas = JAP_japusa_bros_jap
			USA = {
				add_opinion_modifier = {
					target = JAP
					modifier = common_market
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				original_tag = USA
			}
			add_ideas = JAP_japusa_bros_usa
			JAP = {
				add_opinion_modifier = {
					target = USA
					modifier = common_market
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

		}
	}

		ai_chance = {

				factor = 0

		mdmosjap_increase_party_popularity_array_1_var_1 = yes
		mdmosjap_increase_party_popularity_array_2_var_2 = yes

		mdmosjap_increase_party_popularity_array_2_var_1 = yes
		mdmosjap_increase_party_popularity_array_3_var_1 = yes
		mdmosjap_increase_party_popularity_array_18_var_05 = yes
		add_to_variable = {
			var = var_JAP_financial_crisis_recover_date_counts
			value = 100
		}
	}

	#Nothing
	option = {

			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.200916004.oC
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.200916004.oC"

		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = stagnation }
			swap_ideas = { remove_idea = stagnation add_idea = stable_growth }

			limit = { has_idea = recession }
			swap_ideas = { remove_idea = recession add_idea = stagnation }
		}

			limit = { has_idea = depression }
			swap_ideas = { remove_idea = depression add_idea = recession }
		}

	}

		JAP = {
			has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_ZAITOKUKAI
			NOT = { has_government = nationalist }
		}
	}

	option = {

				AND = {

#Boat Collision in Senkaku: Treat of Captain
country_event = {
	id = mdmosjap_japan.220907002
	title = mdmosjap_japan.220907002.t
	desc = mdmosjap_japan.220907002.d
	#picture = GFX_news_event_hearts_of_iron_4

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	#Release the captain
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 90
			modifier = {
				OR = {
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 0 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 1 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 6 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 7 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 13 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 14 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 15 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 20 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 21 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 22 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 23 }
				}
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.220907002.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.220907002.oA"
		CHI = { country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.220907901 days = 15 } }	#2010.09.23
		set_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_SENKAKU_COLLISION_WITHOUT_CAPTAIN
	}

	#Release all sailors.

	#Keep a detention
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				OR = {
					is_historical_focus_on = yes
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 3 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 4 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 5 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 18 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 19 }
				}
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.220907002.oC
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.220907002.oC"
		CHI = { country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.220907903 days = 11 } }	#2010.09.19
		set_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_SENKAKU_COLLISION_DETAIN
	}
}

#The Recorded Video of Senkaku Collision: Treat of Video
country_event = {
	id = mdmosjap_japan.221104001
	title = mdmosjap_japan.221104001.t
	desc = mdmosjap_japan.221104001.d
	#picture = GFX_news_event_hearts_of_iron_4

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		JAP = {
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_SENKAKU_COLLISION_WITHOUT_CAPTAIN
				has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_SENKAKU_COLLISION_WITH_CAPTAIN
				has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_SENKAKU_COLLISION_DETAIN
			}
		}
	}

	#Only show to the Dietpersons
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 90
			modifier = {
				OR = {
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 20 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 21 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 22 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 23 }
				}
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.221104001.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.221104001.oA"
		add_war_support = 0.02
		set_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_SENKAKU_VIDEO_LIMITED
		hidden_effect = { ROOT = { country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.221104002 days = 3 } } }
	}

	#Release the video to public, but edited
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 5
			modifier = {
				OR = {
					is_historical_focus_on = yes
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 20 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 21 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 22 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 23 }
				}
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.221104001.oB
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.221104001.oB"
		add_political_power = -100
		add_war_support = 0.05
		set_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_SENKAKU_VIDEO_EDITED
		hidden_effect = {
			CHI = { country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.221104003 hours = 12 } }
			ROOT = { country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.221104002 days = 3 } }
		}
	}

	#Release the full video to public
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 5
			modifier = {
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.221104001.oC
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.221104001.oC"
		add_political_power = -200
		add_war_support = 0.10
		set_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_SENKAKU_VIDEO_FULL
		hidden_effect = { CHI = { country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.221104003 hours = 12 } } }
	}
}

#The Recorded Video of Senkaku Collision: Sengoku38
country_event = {
	id = mdmosjap_japan.221104002
	title = mdmosjap_japan.221104002.t
	desc = mdmosjap_japan.221104002.d
	#picture = GFX_news_event_hearts_of_iron_4

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = mdmosjap_japan.221104002.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.221104002.oA"
		add_war_support = 0.05
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_SENKAKU_VIDEO_LIMITED }
			mdmosjap_decrease_ruling_party_popularity_6 = yes
			increase_mdmosjap_concon_right_2 = yes
			set_temp_variable = { jap_radical_change = 2 }
			jap_modify_radicalism_right = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_SENKAKU_VIDEO_EDITED }
			mdmosjap_decrease_ruling_party_popularity_3 = yes
			increase_mdmosjap_concon_right_1 = yes
			set_temp_variable = { jap_radical_change = 1 }
			jap_modify_radicalism_right = yes
		}
		if = { limit = { NOT = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 6 } } } mdmosjap_increase_party_popularity_array_6_var_2 = yes }
		if = { limit = { NOT = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 7 } } } mdmosjap_increase_party_popularity_array_7_var_2 = yes }
		if = { limit = { NOT = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 20 } } } mdmosjap_increase_party_popularity_array_20_var_2 = yes }
		if = { limit = { NOT = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 21 } } } mdmosjap_increase_party_popularity_array_21_var_2 = yes }
		if = { limit = { NOT = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 22 } } } mdmosjap_increase_party_popularity_array_22_var_2 = yes }
		JAP = { country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japannews.221104101 days = 2 } }
		news_event = { id = mdmosjap_japannews.221104002 days = 1 }
	}
}

#Statue of Peace: Koreans in USA established Confort Woman's Statue
country_event = {
	id = mdmosjap_japan.250730001
	title = mdmosjap_japan.250730001.t
	desc = mdmosjap_japan.250730001.d
	#picture = GFX_news_event_hearts_of_iron_4

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	#Protest
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				OR = {
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 3 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 4 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 5 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 17 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 18 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 19 }
				}
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.250730001.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.250730001.oA"
		mdmosjap_increase_party_popularity_array_0_var_2 = yes
		mdmosjap_increase_party_popularity_array_1_var_2 = yes
		mdmosjap_increase_party_popularity_array_6_var_2 = yes
		mdmosjap_increase_party_popularity_array_7_var_2 = yes
		mdmosjap_increase_party_popularity_array_13_var_2 = yes
		mdmosjap_increase_party_popularity_array_15_var_2 = yes
		mdmosjap_increase_party_popularity_array_20_var_1 = yes
		mdmosjap_increase_party_popularity_array_21_var_1 = yes
		set_temp_variable = { jap_radical_change = 2 }
		jap_modify_radicalism_left = yes
		set_temp_variable = { jap_radical_change = 1 }
		jap_modify_radicalism_right = yes
		KOR = { country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.250730002 days = 1 } }
		USA = { country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.250730003 days = 1 } }
		if = {
			limit = { JAP = { has_opinion_modifier = mdmosjap_opinion_KOR_statue_of_peace_2 } }
			hidden_effect = {
				remove_opinion_modifier = { target = KOR modifier = mdmosjap_opinion_KOR_statue_of_peace_2 }
				add_opinion_modifier = { target = KOR modifier = mdmosjap_opinion_KOR_statue_of_peace_3 }
			}
			set_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_OPINION_MODIFIER_JAP_KOR_DIPLOMATIC_CONFLICT
		}
		if = {
			limit = { JAP = { has_opinion_modifier = mdmosjap_opinion_KOR_statue_of_peace_1 } }
			hidden_effect = {
				remove_opinion_modifier = { target = KOR modifier = mdmosjap_opinion_KOR_statue_of_peace_1 }
				add_opinion_modifier = { target = KOR modifier = mdmosjap_opinion_KOR_statue_of_peace_2 }
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = MDMOSJAP_OPINION_MODIFIER_ANTI_SOUTH_KOREA_FOR_STATUE_TT
	}

	#Accept
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				OR = {
					is_historical_focus_on = yes
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 0 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 1 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 6 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 7 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 13 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 14 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 15 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 20 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 21 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 22 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 23 }
				}
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.250730001.oB
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.250730001.oB"
		mdmosjap_increase_party_popularity_array_2_var_2 = yes
		mdmosjap_increase_party_popularity_array_3_var_2 = yes
		mdmosjap_increase_party_popularity_array_4_var_1 = yes
		mdmosjap_increase_party_popularity_array_5_var_1 = yes
		mdmosjap_increase_party_popularity_array_14_var_2 = yes
		mdmosjap_increase_party_popularity_array_17_var_2 = yes
		mdmosjap_increase_party_popularity_array_18_var_2 = yes
		mdmosjap_increase_party_popularity_array_19_var_1 = yes
		set_temp_variable = { jap_radical_change = 1 }
		jap_modify_radicalism_left = yes
		set_temp_variable = { jap_radical_change = 2 }

		custom_effect_tooltip = MDMOSJAP_RETIREMENT_TAKAKO_DOI_TT
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_leader = { name = "Takako Doi" } }
			kill_country_leader = yes
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Interim Cabinet" picture = "leader_the_diet.dds" ideology = socialism
				traits = { interim_cabinet }
			}
			add_stability = -0.02

			changepm_mdmosjap_JAP_candidates_remedy_for_SDP = yes	#Remedy for vacancy of candidates on the SDP

			changepm_mdmosjap_JAP_addflag_resignation = yes			#Make a flag for the resignation of P.M.
			changepm_mdmosjap_JAP_prime_minister_election = yes		#Choose the next Prime Minister
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = mdmosjap_japan.340201001
	title = mdmosjap_japan.340201001.t
	desc = mdmosjap_japan.340201001.d
	#picture = GFX_news_event_hearts_of_iron_4

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	#He was the Father of Racism
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 90
			modifier = {
				OR = {
				#	trigger_mdmosjap_has_the_rightwing_government = yes
					has_country_leader = { name = "Shinzo Abe" }
				}
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.340201001.oB
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.340201001.oB"
		set_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_RETIREMENT_SHINTARO_ISHIHARA
		custom_effect_tooltip = MDMOSJAP_RETIREMENT_SHINTARO_ISHIHARA_TT
		set_temp_variable = { jap_radical_change = 4 }
		jap_modify_radicalism_right = yes
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_leader = { name = "Shintaro Ishihara" } }
			kill_country_leader = yes
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Interim Cabinet" picture = "leader_the_diet.dds" ideology = conservatism
				traits = { interim_cabinet }
			}

			changepm_mdmosjap_JAP_addflag_resignation = yes			#Make a flag for the resignation of P.M.
			changepm_mdmosjap_JAP_prime_minister_election = yes		#Choose the next Prime Minister
		}
	}

	#No comment
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 5
			modifier = {
				OR = {
					trigger_mdmosjap_has_the_leftwing_government = yes
					trigger_mdmosjap_has_the_centrist_government = yes
					trigger_mdmosjap_has_the_islamist_government = yes
				}
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.340201001.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.340201001.oA"
		set_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_RETIREMENT_SHINTARO_ISHIHARA
		custom_effect_tooltip = MDMOSJAP_RETIREMENT_SHINTARO_ISHIHARA_TT
		increase_mdmosjap_concon_right_2 = yes
		set_temp_variable = { jap_radical_change = 2 }
		jap_modify_radicalism_left = yes
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_leader = { name = "Shintaro Ishihara" } }
			kill_country_leader = yes
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Interim Cabinet" picture = "leader_the_diet.dds" ideology = conservatism
				traits = { interim_cabinet }
			}

			changepm_mdmosjap_JAP_addflag_resignation = yes			#Make a flag for the resignation of P.M.
			changepm_mdmosjap_JAP_prime_minister_election = yes		#Choose the next Prime Minister
		}
	}
}

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

		JAP = {
			has_government = democratic
			OR = {
				has_country_leader = { name = "Keizo Obuchi" }
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		set_variable = { mdmosjap_2000_ldp_lp_negotiation_rejected_count = 0 }
		set_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_KATO_REBELLION_LOADED
	}

	#Obuchi compromised with the taxation-based system
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan_kato.51.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan_kato.51.oA"
		add_political_power = -20
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan_kato.52 days = 21 }
		}
	}

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan_kato.51.oB
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan_kato.51.oB"
		add_political_power = 20
		add_to_variable = { mdmosjap_2000_ldp_lp_negotiation_rejected_count = 1 }
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan_kato.52 days = 21 }
		}
	}
}

#[HIDDEN] Obuchi-Ozawa Negotiation Result Check
country_event = {
	id = mdmosjap_japan_kato.54
	hidden = yes

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		set_variable = { mdmosjap_2000_ldp_lp_negotiation_rejected_penalty = mdmosjap_2000_ldp_lp_negotiation_rejected_count }
		multiply_variable = { mdmosjap_2000_ldp_lp_negotiation_rejected_penalty = -150 }
	}


	option = {
		name = mdmosjap_japan_kato.54.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan_kato.54.oA"
		if = {			#Collapse of Ji-Ji-Ko Coalition
			limit = {
				OR = {
					check_variable = { mdmosjap_2000_ldp_lp_negotiation_rejected_count > 2 }
					check_variable = { mdmosjap_2000_ldp_lp_negotiation_rejected_count = 2 }
					has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_2000_LDP_LP_NEGOTIATION_CONTRAINDICANT_OPTION
				}
			}
			country_event = mdmosjap_japan_kato.55
		} else = {		#LP Remains in the Coalition
			country_event = mdmosjap_japan_kato.56
		}
	}
}

#Collapse of Ji-Ji-Ko Coalition (Kato Rebellion Series)

	}

		set_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_LP
		hidden_effect = { recalculate_party = yes update_government_coalition_strength = yes update_party_name = yes set_coalition_drift = yes }

#[HIDDEN] Election Result Check
country_event = {
	id = mdmosjap_japan_kato.15
	hidden = yes

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	#LDP Lost The Election
	option = {
		trigger = {
			NOT = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 0 } }
			NOT = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 1 } }
			NOT = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 7 } }
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan_kato.15.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan_kato.15.oA"
		country_event = mdmosjap_japan_kato.16
	}

	#LDP Won The Election
	option = {
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				is_in_array = { ruling_party = 0 }
				is_in_array = { ruling_party = 1 }
				is_in_array = { ruling_party = 7 }
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan_kato.15.oB
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan_kato.15.oB"
		country_event = mdmosjap_japan_kato.17
	}
}

			original_tag = RYU

			NOT = { has_war = yes }
			has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_NF_JAPAN_JROTC_FURUSATO_GUARDS_AVAILABLE
			NOT = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_NF_JAPAN_JROTC_FURUSATO_GUARDS_DEBUG_ENABLED }
		}
	}

		delete_unit_template_and_units = { division_template = "Furusato Guards" disband = yes }

				limit = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_NF_JAPAN_JROTC_FURUSATO_GUARDS_ASSEMBLED_IN_CHUBU }
				clr_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_NF_JAPAN_JROTC_FURUSATO_GUARDS_ASSEMBLED_IN_CHUBU

				limit = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_NF_JAPAN_JROTC_FURUSATO_GUARDS_ASSEMBLED_IN_KINKI }
				clr_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_NF_JAPAN_JROTC_FURUSATO_GUARDS_ASSEMBLED_IN_KINKI

				clr_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_NF_JAPAN_JROTC_FURUSATO_GUARDS_ASSEMBLED_IN_CHUGOKU

#Constitutional Contradiction
country_event = {
	id = mdmosjap_japan.1511801
	title = mdmosjap_japan.1511801.t
	desc = mdmosjap_japan.1511801.d
	#picture = GFX_news_event_hearts_of_iron_4

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
	}

	option = {
		name = mdmosjap_japan.1511801.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.1511801.oA"
		swap_ideas = { remove_idea = JAP_holy_article_9 add_idea = JAP_holy_article_9contradicted1 }
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = intervention_isolation }
			swap_ideas = { remove_idea = intervention_isolation add_idea = intervention_regional_interventionism }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = intervention_local_security }
			swap_ideas = { remove_idea = intervention_local_security add_idea = intervention_regional_interventionism }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = intervention_limited_interventionism }
			swap_ideas = { remove_idea = intervention_limited_interventionism add_idea = intervention_regional_interventionism }
		}
		increase_mdmosjap_concon_left_3 = yes
		set_temp_variable = { jap_radical_change = 3 }
		jap_modify_radicalism_left = yes
	}
}

	is_triggered_only = yes

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
			modifier = {
				AND = {
					NOT = { tag = USA }
					JAP = { NOT = { has_elections = yes } }
				}
				factor = 0.5
			}
			modifier = {
				AND = {
					NOT = { tag = USA }
					JAP = { has_government = nationalist }
				}
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.1601701.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.1601701.oA"
		JAP = { country_event = mdmosjap_japan.1601702 }
	}

	#We refuse
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
			modifier = {
				AND = {
					NOT = { tag = USA }
					JAP = { NOT = { has_elections = yes } }
				}
				add = 5
			}
			modifier = {
				AND = {
					NOT = { tag = USA }
					JAP = { NOT = { has_government = democratic } }
				}
				add = 5
			}
			modifier = {
				AND = {
					NOT = { tag = USA }
					JAP = { has_government = nationalist }
				}
				add = 25
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.1601701.oB
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.1601701.oB"
		JAP = { country_event = mdmosjap_japan.1601703 }
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = mdmosjap_japan.91650101
	title = mdmosjap_japan.91650101.t
	desc = mdmosjap_japan.91650101.d
	#picture = GFX_news_event_hearts_of_iron_4

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	#Accept Japan's Demand
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 95
			modifier = {
				FROM = {
					OR = {
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 4 }
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 5 }
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 18 }
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 19 }
					}
				}
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.91650101.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.91650101.oA"
		add_political_power = -50
		FROM = { country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.91650102 days = 1 } }
	}

	#Reject Japan's Demand
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 5
			modifier = {
				FROM = {
					OR = {
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 0 }
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 1 }
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 2 }
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 3 }
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 6 }
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 7 }
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 13 }
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 15 }
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 16 }
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 17 }
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 20 }
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 21 }
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 22 }
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 23 }
					}
				}
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.91650101.oB
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.91650101.oB"
		add_political_power = -100
		FROM = { country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.91650103 days = 1 } }
	}
}

#U.S. Accepts the Right of Investigation
country_event = {
	id = mdmosjap_japan.91650102
	title = mdmosjap_japan.91650102.t
	desc = mdmosjap_japan.91650102.d
	#picture = GFX_news_event_hearts_of_iron_4

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = mdmosjap_japan.91650102.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.91650102.oA"
		add_political_power = 100
		mdmosjap_increase_ruling_party_popularity_5 = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 2 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 3 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 4 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 5 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 16 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 17 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 18 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 19 }
				}
			}
			set_temp_variable = { jap_radical_change = -1 }
			jap_modify_radicalism_left = yes
			set_temp_variable = { jap_radical_change = 5 }
			jap_modify_radicalism_right = yes

		} else_if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 6 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 7 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 20 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 21 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 22 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 23 }
				}
			}
			set_temp_variable = { jap_radical_change = 5 }
			jap_modify_radicalism_left = yes
			set_temp_variable = { jap_radical_change = -1 }
			jap_modify_radicalism_right = yes
		} else = {
			set_temp_variable = { jap_radical_change = -3 }
			jap_modify_radicalism_left = yes
			set_temp_variable = { jap_radical_change = -3 }
			jap_modify_radicalism_right = yes
		}
		increase_mdmosjap_concon_right_2 = yes
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = mdmosjap_japan.1620201
	title = mdmosjap_japan.1620201.t
	desc = mdmosjap_japan.1620201.d
	#picture = GFX_news_event_hearts_of_iron_4

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	#LDP, JIP or Nationalists
	option = {
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				is_in_array = { ruling_party = 0 }
				is_in_array = { ruling_party = 1 }
				is_in_array = { ruling_party = 6 }
				is_in_array = { ruling_party = 7 }
				has_government = nationalist
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.1620201.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.1620201.oA"
		USA = { country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.1620202 hours = 1 } }
		KOR = { country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.1620203 hours = 1 } }
		TAI = { country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.1620203 hours = 1 } }
		CHI = { country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.1620204 hours = 1 } }
		NKO = { country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.1620204 hours = 1 } }
		SOV = { country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.1620204 hours = 1 } }
		news_event = { id = mdmosjap_japannews.1620201 days = 1 }
	}

	#Not LDP, JIP and Nationalists
	option = {
		trigger = {
			AND = {
				NOT = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 0 } }
				NOT = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 1 } }
				NOT = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 6 } }
				NOT = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 7 } }
				NOT = { has_government = nationalist }
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.1620201.oB
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.1620201.oB"
		USA = { country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.1620202 hours = 1 } }
		KOR = { country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.1620203 hours = 1 } }
		TAI = { country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.1620203 hours = 1 } }
		CHI = { country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.1620204 hours = 1 } }
		NKO = { country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.1620204 hours = 1 } }
		SOV = { country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.1620204 hours = 1 } }
		news_event = { id = mdmosjap_japannews.1620201 days = 1 }
		#"Loopy" hooting
		JAP = { country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.1620205 days = 3 } }
		#SDP gets angry
		if = {
			limit = { is_in_array = { gov_coalition_array = 3 } }
			JAP = { country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.1620206 days = 6 } }
		}
	}
}

			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				check_variable = { var = mdmosjap_JAP_var_HenokoNegotiation value = 6 compare = less_than }
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.1640206.oA
		JAP = { country_event = mdmosjap_japan.1640207 }
		ROOT = { add_opinion_modifier = { target = JAP modifier = recent_actions_positive } }
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.1640206.oA"
	}

	#We Cannot Agree This Plan
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				check_variable = { var = mdmosjap_JAP_var_HenokoNegotiation value = 6 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.1640206.oB
		JAP = { country_event = mdmosjap_japan.1640208 }
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.1640206.oB"
	}
}

#Henoko Negotiation: The United States Agreed
country_event = {
	id = mdmosjap_japan.1640207
	title = mdmosjap_japan.1640207.t
	desc = mdmosjap_japan.1640207.d
	#picture = GFX_news_event_hearts_of_iron_4

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = mdmosjap_japan.generic_great
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.1640207.oA"
		#By the Withdrawal Proposal
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_HENOKO_NEGOTIATION_SMALL_WITHDRAWAL }
			827 = { remove_building = { type = air_base level = mdmosjap_JAP_var_HenokoNegotiation_moving } }
			618 = { add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_HENOKO_NEGOTIATION_MEDIUM_WITHDRAWAL }
			827 = { remove_building = { type = air_base level = mdmosjap_JAP_var_HenokoNegotiation_moving } }
			618 = { add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 2 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_HENOKO_NEGOTIATION_LARGE_WITHDRAWAL }
			827 = { remove_building = { type = air_base level = mdmosjap_JAP_var_HenokoNegotiation_moving } }
			618 = { add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 3 }
		}

		#By the Allotment Proposal
		if = {
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_HenokoNegotiation_debt > 0 } }
				add_to_variable = { debt = mdmosjap_JAP_var_HenokoNegotiation_debt }
				custom_effect_tooltip = MDMOSJAP_add_debt_HenokoNegotiation_TT
				set_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EXTERNAL_DEBT_CHANGE
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_HenokoNegotiation_debt = 0 } }
				custom_effect_tooltip = MDMOSJAP_add_debt_HenokoNegotiation_zero_TT
			}
			clear_variable = mdmosjap_JAP_var_HenokoNegotiation_debt
		}

		#By the Replace Location
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_HENOKO_NEGOTIATION_MOVE_TO_TOHOKU }
			divide_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_HenokoNegotiation_moving = 2 }
			617 = { add_building_construction = { type = air_base level = mdmosjap_JAP_var_HenokoNegotiation_moving instant_build = yes } }
			616 = { add_building_construction = { type = air_base level = mdmosjap_JAP_var_HenokoNegotiation_moving instant_build = yes } }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_HENOKO_NEGOTIATION_MOVE_TO_CHUBU }
			613 = { add_building_construction = { type = air_base level = mdmosjap_JAP_var_HenokoNegotiation_moving instant_build = yes } }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_HENOKO_NEGOTIATION_MOVE_TO_SHIKOKU }
			divide_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_HenokoNegotiation_moving = 2 }
			611 = { add_building_construction = { type = air_base level = mdmosjap_JAP_var_HenokoNegotiation_moving instant_build = yes } }
			610 = { add_building_construction = { type = air_base level = mdmosjap_JAP_var_HenokoNegotiation_moving instant_build = yes } }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_HENOKO_NEGOTIATION_MOVE_TO_IWOJIMA }
			divide_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_HenokoNegotiation_moving = 2 }
			621 = { add_building_construction = { type = air_base level = mdmosjap_JAP_var_HenokoNegotiation_moving instant_build = yes } }
			620 = { add_building_construction = { type = air_base level = mdmosjap_JAP_var_HenokoNegotiation_moving instant_build = yes } }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_HENOKO_NEGOTIATION_MOVE_AND_TRANSFER }
			divide_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_HenokoNegotiation_moving = 2 }
			621 = { add_building_construction = { type = air_base level = mdmosjap_JAP_var_HenokoNegotiation_moving instant_build = yes } }
			620 = { add_building_construction = { type = air_base level = mdmosjap_JAP_var_HenokoNegotiation_moving instant_build = yes } }
			JAP = { country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.1640209 days = 1 } }	#Transfer Event
		}
		clear_variable = mdmosjap_JAP_var_HenokoNegotiation
		clear_variable = mdmosjap_JAP_var_HenokoNegotiation_moving
		ROOT = { add_opinion_modifier = { target = USA modifier = recent_actions_very_positive } }
		add_country_leader_trait = honest
		set_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_HENOKO_NEGOTIATION_AGREED
	}
}

#Claiming the Land in Okinawa
country_event = {
	id = mdmosjap_japan.1660201
	title = mdmosjap_japan.1660201.t
	desc = mdmosjap_japan.1660201.d
	#picture = GFX_news_event_hearts_of_iron_4

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	#Promise Japan's Demand
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 90
			modifier = {
				FROM = {
					OR = {
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 4 }
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 5 }
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 18 }
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 19 }
					}
				}
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.1660201.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.1660201.oA"
		add_political_power = -100
		add_ideas = JAP_USA_base_removal_in_okinawa1
		827 = { set_demilitarized_zone = yes }
		FROM = { country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.1660202 days = 1 } }
		effect_tooltip = { JAP = { add_opinion_modifier = { target = USA modifier = mdmosjap_opinion_USA_JAP_base_removal_promised } } }
	}

	#Reject Japan's Demand
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				FROM = {
					OR = {
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 0 }
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 1 }
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 2 }
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 3 }
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 6 }
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 7 }
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 13 }
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 15 }
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 16 }
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 17 }
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 20 }
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 21 }
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 22 }
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 23 }
					}
				}
				factor = 0
			}
			modifier = {
				OR = {
					any_country = {
						original_tag = CHI
						OR = {
							has_war_with = JAP
							has_war_with = USA
							has_war_with = TAI
							has_war_with = VIE
							has_war_with = PHI
							has_war_with = MAY
							has_war_with = IND
							has_war_with = RAJ
						}
					}
					any_country = {
						original_tag = NKO
						OR = {
							has_war_with = JAP
							has_war_with = USA
							has_war_with = KOR
						}
					}
					any_country = {
						original_tag = SOV
						OR = {
							has_war_with = JAP
							has_war_with = USA
							has_war_with = FIN
							has_war_with = SWE
							has_war_with = FRA
							has_war_with = GER
							has_war_with = ENG
							has_war_with = UKR
						}
					}
					AND = {
						OR = {
							tag = TAI
							tag = KOR
						}
						exists = no
					}
				}
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.1660201.oB
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.1660201.oB"
		add_political_power = -200
		effect_tooltip = { JAP = { add_opinion_modifier = { target = USA modifier = mdmosjap_opinion_USA_JAP_base_removal_rejected } } }
		FROM = { country_event = mdmosjap_japan.1660203 }
	}
}

#U.S. Promises to return the land in Okinawa
country_event = {
	id = mdmosjap_japan.1660202
	title = mdmosjap_japan.1660202.t
	desc = mdmosjap_japan.1660202.d
	#picture = GFX_news_event_hearts_of_iron_4

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		set_variable = { mdmosjap_var_futenma_returning_stage = 0 }
		set_variable = { mdmosjap_var_futenma_returning_stage_tt = 5 }
	}

	option = {
		name = mdmosjap_japan.1660202.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.1660202.oA"
		add_political_power = 100
		mdmosjap_increase_ruling_party_popularity_5 = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 2 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 3 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 4 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 5 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 16 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 17 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 18 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 19 }
				}
			}
			set_temp_variable = { jap_radical_change = -1 }
			jap_modify_radicalism_left = yes
			set_temp_variable = { jap_radical_change = 5 }
			jap_modify_radicalism_right = yes

		} else_if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 6 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 7 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 20 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 21 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 22 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 23 }
				}
			}
			set_temp_variable = { jap_radical_change = 5 }
			jap_modify_radicalism_left = yes
			set_temp_variable = { jap_radical_change = -1 }
			jap_modify_radicalism_right = yes
		} else = {
			set_temp_variable = { jap_radical_change = -3 }
			jap_modify_radicalism_left = yes
			set_temp_variable = { jap_radical_change = -3 }
			jap_modify_radicalism_right = yes
		}
		increase_mdmosjap_concon_right_2 = yes
		add_ideas = JAP_base_removal_in_okinawa1
		set_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_NF_RECLAIM_FUTENMA_USA_PROMISED
		add_opinion_modifier = { target = USA modifier = mdmosjap_opinion_USA_JAP_base_removal_promised }
		activate_mission = mdmosjap_JAP_retreat_of_usfj
		hidden_effect = { news_event = mdmosjap_japannews.1660202 }
	}
}

#U.S. has returned the land in Okinawa
country_event = {
	id = mdmosjap_japan.1660205
	title = mdmosjap_japan.1660205.t
	desc = mdmosjap_japan.1660205.d
	#picture = GFX_news_event_hearts_of_iron_4

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = mdmosjap_japan.1660205.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.1660205.oA"
		USA = {
			remove_state_core = 827
		}
		JAP = {
			transfer_state = 827
			add_state_core = 827
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = JAP_base_removal_in_okinawa1 }
			remove_ideas = JAP_base_removal_in_okinawa1
		}
		if = {	#Support limitedly
			limit = { has_idea = JAP_base_removal_in_okinawa2 }
			remove_ideas = JAP_base_removal_in_okinawa2
			add_timed_idea = { idea = JAP_base_removal_in_okinawa_localsupport1 days = 1825 }
		}
		if = {	#Support fully
			limit = { has_idea = JAP_base_removal_in_okinawa3 }
			remove_ideas = JAP_base_removal_in_okinawa3
			add_timed_idea = { idea = JAP_base_removal_in_okinawa_localsupport2 days = 1825 }
		}
		set_temp_variable = { mdmosjap_temp_var_futenma_new_building_slot = 0 }
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_NF_RECLAIM_FUTENMA_RETURN_EVERY_LANDS }
			add_to_temp_variable = { mdmosjap_temp_var_futenma_new_building_slot = 1 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_NF_RECLAIM_FUTENMA_RETURN_EVERY_LANDS } }
			add_to_temp_variable = { mdmosjap_temp_var_futenma_new_building_slot = 2 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_NF_RECLAIM_FUTENMA_FUTENMA_REDEVELOPMENT }
			827 = {
				custom_effect_tooltip = MDMOSJAP_NF_RECLAIM_FUTENMA_DESTROY_ALL_MILIFACILITIES_TT
				hidden_effect = {
					if = {
						limit = { dockyard > 0 }
						remove_building = { type = dockyard level = 99 }
					}
					if = {
						limit = { arms_factory > 0 }
						remove_building = { type = arms_factory level = 99 }
					}
					if = {
						limit = { air_base > 0 }
						remove_building = { type = air_base level = 99 }
					}
					if = {
						limit = { radar_station > 0 }
						remove_building = { type = radar_station level = 99 }
					}
					if = {
						limit = { anti_air_building > 0 }
						remove_building = { type = anti_air_building level = 99 }
					}
					if = {
						limit = { missile_defense_station > 0 }
						remove_building = { type = missile_defense_station level = 99 }
					}
					if = {
						limit = { TEL_base > 0 }
						remove_building = { type = TEL_base level = 99 }
					}
					if = {
						limit = { missile_silo > 0 }
						remove_building = { type = missile_silo level = 99 }
					}
					if = {
						limit = { nuclear_reactor > 0 }
						remove_building = { type = nuclear_reactor level = 99 }
					}
					if = {
						limit = { fuel_silo > 0 }
						remove_building = { type = fuel_silo level = 99 }
					}
				}
			}
			add_to_temp_variable = { mdmosjap_temp_var_futenma_new_building_slot = 2 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_NF_RECLAIM_FUTENMA_FUTENMA_JASDF_AIR_BASE }
			827 = {
				custom_effect_tooltip = MDMOSJAP_NF_RECLAIM_FUTENMA_REMAIN_SOME_MILIFACILITIES_TT
				hidden_effect = {
					if = {
						limit = { dockyard > 0 }
						remove_building = { type = dockyard level = 99 }
					}
					if = {
						limit = { arms_factory > 0 }
						remove_building = { type = arms_factory level = 99 }
					}
					if = {
						limit = { missile_silo > 0 }
						remove_building = { type = missile_silo level = 99 }
					}
					if = {
						limit = { nuclear_reactor > 0 }
						remove_building = { type = nuclear_reactor level = 99 }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		827 = {
			add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = mdmosjap_temp_var_futenma_new_building_slot
			set_state_name = mdmosjap_rename_STATE_827
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { is_core_of = RYU } }
				hidden_effect = { add_core_of = RYU }
			}
		}
		set_province_name = { id = 7115 name = mdmosjap_rename_VICTORY_POINT_7115 }
		set_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_NF_RECLAIM_FUTENMA_USA_HAS_WITHDRAWN
		remove_mission = mdmosjap_JAP_retreat_of_usfj
		hidden_effect = { news_event = mdmosjap_japannews.1660205 }
	}
}

			remove_ideas = JAP_base_removal_in_okinawa3

			}

		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.1660209.oB"
		add_stability = -0.01
		add_opinion_modifier = { target = FROM modifier = mdmosjap_opinion_USA_JAP_broken_promise_by_war_month }
		effect_tooltip = { remove_mission = mdmosjap_JAP_retreat_of_usfj }

#The Fate of Futenma Base
country_event = {
	id = mdmosjap_japan.1604001
	title = mdmosjap_japan.1604001.t
	desc = mdmosjap_japan.1604001.d
	#picture = GFX_news_event_hearts_of_iron_4

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	#Demand the restitution of Futenma (Add 2 Slots into Okinawa State)
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				OR = {
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 0 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 1 }
				}
				factor = 0.02
			}
			modifier = {
				OR = {
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 6 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 7 }
				}
				factor = 0
			}
			modifier = {
				AND = {
					has_completed_focus = JAP_china_encirclement
					CHI = {
						AND = {
							exists = yes
							is_puppet = no
							is_subject = no
							NOT = { is_in_faction_with = ROOT }
						}
					}
				}
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.1604001.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.1604001.oA"
		USA = { country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.1604002 days = 1 } }
	}

	#Ask the United States to maintain there as the U.S.F.J. base
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				is_in_array = { ruling_party = 2 }
				factor = 0.1
			}
			modifier = {
				OR = {
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 3 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 4 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 5 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 18 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 19 }
					has_government = nationalist
				}
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.1604001.oB
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.1604001.oB"
		USA = { country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.1604005 days = 1 } }
	}
}

	id = mdmosjap_japan.1604002
	title = mdmosjap_japan.1604002.t
	desc = mdmosjap_japan.1604002.d
	#picture = GFX_news_event_hearts_of_iron_4

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	#Accpet to Return
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				FROM = {
					OR = {
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 4 }
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 5 }
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 18 }
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 19 }
						has_government = nationalist
					}
				}
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.1604002.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.1604002.oA"
		FROM = {
			transfer_state = 827
			add_state_core = 827
		}
		ROOT = {
			remove_state_core = 827
		}
		FROM = { country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.1604003 } }
	}

	#Refuse to Return
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				OR = {
					CHI = {
						AND = {
							exists = yes
							is_puppet = no
							is_subject = no
							NOT = { is_in_faction_with = ROOT }
						}
					}
					RYU = {
						AND = {
							exists = yes
							OR = {
								NOT = { is_puppet_of = CHI }
								NOT = { is_subject_of = CHI }
							}
						}
					}
					ROOT = { has_completed_focus = USA_seek_proximity_to_china }
				}
				factor = 0
			}
			modifier = {
				FROM = {
					NOT = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 4 } }
					NOT = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 5 } }
					NOT = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 18 } }
					NOT = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 19 } }
					NOT = { has_government = nationalist }
				}
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.1604002.oB
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.1604002.oB"
		add_political_power = -100
		FROM = { country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.1604004 } }
	}
}

		set_temp_variable = { jap_radical_change = -10 }
		jap_modify_radicalism_left = yes
		set_temp_variable = { jap_radical_change = -5 }
		jap_modify_radicalism_right = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				RYU = {
					exists = yes
					NOT = { is_puppet_of = FROM }
					NOT = { is_subject_of = FROM }
				}
			}
			hidden_effect = { RYU = { country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.1604008 days = 2 } } }
		}
	}
}

#Japan Refused to Return Futenma!
country_event = {
	id = mdmosjap_japan.1604011
	title = mdmosjap_japan.1604011.t
	desc = mdmosjap_japan.1604011.d
	#picture = GFX_news_event_hearts_of_iron_4

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	#We never forget this (but do nothing)
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.1604011.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.1604011.oA"
		add_political_power = -200
		add_war_support = 0.05
		if = {
			limit = { has_government = nationalist }
			add_popularity = { ideology = democratic popularity = 0.05 }
		}
	}

	#Now we will take our land by force (Gain the Casus Belli)
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				any_other_country = {
					AND = {
						is_in_faction_with = ROOT
						is_major = no
					}
				}
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.1604011.oB
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.1604012.oB"
		add_political_power = -200
		add_war_support = 0.05
		if = {
			limit = { has_government = nationalist }
			add_popularity = { ideology = democratic popularity = 0.05 }
		}
		create_wargoal = { type = take_state_focus target = FROM generator = { 827 } }
	}

country_event = {
	id = mdmosjap_japan.1610901
	title = mdmosjap_japan.1610901.t
	desc = mdmosjap_japan.1610901.d
	#picture = GFX_news_event_hearts_of_iron_4

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	#We sign this.
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 90
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.1610901.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.1610901.oA"
		JAP = { country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.1610902 days = 1 } }
	}

	#We never sign this.
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				JAP = {
					OR = {
						has_government = nationalist
						is_in_faction_with = KOR
					}
				}
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.1610901.oB
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.1610901.oB"
		JAP = { country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.1610903 days = 1 } }
	}
}

#North Korea Accept the Peace Treaty!
country_event = {
	id = mdmosjap_japan.1610902
	title = mdmosjap_japan.1610902.t
	desc = mdmosjap_japan.1610902.d
	#picture = GFX_news_event_hearts_of_iron_4

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = mdmosjap_japan.generic_great
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.1610902.oA"
		if = {
			limit = { NKO = { has_government = democratic } }
			add_popularity = { ideology = democratic popularity = 0.05 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					NKO = { has_government = communism }
					NKO = { has_government = nationalist }
				}
			}
			add_popularity = { ideology = communism popularity = 0.05 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { NKO = { has_government = fascism } }
			add_popularity = { ideology = fascism popularity = 0.05 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					NKO = { has_government = neutrality }
					NKO = { has_government = nationalist }
				}
			}
			add_popularity = { ideology = neutrality popularity = 0.05 }
		}
		mdmosjap_increase_ruling_party_popularity_5 = yes
		if = {
			limit = { JAP = { has_opinion_modifier = mdmosjap_opinion_abduction1 } }
			JAP = { remove_opinion_modifier = { target = JAP modifier = mdmosjap_opinion_abduction1 } }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { JAP = { has_opinion_modifier = mdmosjap_opinion_abduction1 } }
			JAP = { remove_opinion_modifier = { target = JAP modifier = mdmosjap_opinion_abduction2 } }
		}
		NKO = {
			remove_opinion_modifier = { target = JAP modifier = mdmosjap_opinion_recognise_south }
			add_opinion_modifier = { target = JAP modifier = mdmosjap_opinion_NKO_JAP_peace_treaty_approved }
		}
		JAP = { add_opinion_modifier = { target = NKO modifier = mdmosjap_opinion_NKO_JAP_peace_treaty_approved } }
		KOR = { add_opinion_modifier = { target = JAP modifier = mdmosjap_opinion_recognise_north } }
		add_stability = 0.05
		add_war_support = -0.05
		remove_ideas = JAP_abductionleague
		JAP = { country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.1610904 days = 1 } }
		news_event = mdmosjap_japannews.1610902
		set_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_JAPNKO_PEACE_TREATY_ACCEPTED
	}
}

			add_manpower = -20000
		}
		if = {
			limit = { JAP = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_JAPKOR_REFUGEE_AGREEMENT_40000 } }
			add_manpower = -40000
		}
		country_event = mdmosjap_japan.1630922
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = mdmosjap_japan.1770802
	title = mdmosjap_japan.1770802.t
	desc = mdmosjap_japan.1770802.d
	#picture = GFX_news_event_hearts_of_iron_4

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		effect_tooltip = {
			if = {
				limit = { FROM = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_NF_AMITY_OIL_FIELD_TAI_INTERESTS_SMALL } }
				random_owned_state = {
					limit = { is_capital = yes }
					add_resource = { type = oil amount = 2 }
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { FROM = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_NF_AMITY_OIL_FIELD_TAI_INTERESTS_MIDDLE } }
				random_owned_state = {
					limit = { is_capital = yes }
					add_resource = { type = oil amount = 4 }
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { FROM = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_NF_AMITY_OIL_FIELD_TAI_INTERESTS_LARGE } }
				random_owned_state = {
					limit = { is_capital = yes }
					add_resource = { type = oil amount = 8 }
				}
			}
		}
	}

	#Accept their offer
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.1770802.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.1770802.oA"
		FROM = { country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.1770803 days = 1 } }
	}

	#Refuse and keep our claim
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				FROM = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_NF_AMITY_OIL_FIELD_TAI_INTERESTS_SMALL }
				add = 100
			}
			modifier = {
				FROM = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_NF_AMITY_OIL_FIELD_TAI_INTERESTS_MIDDLE }
				add = 25
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.1770802.oB
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.1770802.oB"
		FROM = { country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.1770805 days = 1 } }
	}
}

#Japan Requests the South Korean Support
country_event = {
	id = mdmosjap_japan.1682302
	title = mdmosjap_japan.1682302.t
	desc = mdmosjap_japan.1682302.d
	#picture = GFX_news_event_hearts_of_iron_4

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	#Agree the request
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 40
			modifier = {
				AND = {
					ROOT = {
						OR = {
							has_idea = NATO_member
							has_idea = Major_Non_NATO_Ally
						}
					}
					JAP = {
						OR = {
							has_idea = NATO_member
							has_idea = Major_Non_NATO_Ally
						}
					}
				}
				factor = 2
			}
			modifier = {
				JAP = { has_completed_focus = JAP_anti_korea_doctrine }
				factor = 0.5
			}
			modifier = {
				JAP = { has_government = nationalist }
				factor = 0.5
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.1682302.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.1682302.oA"
		set_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_NF_ANTICCP_KOR_SUPPORT_ACCEPTED
		JAP = { country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.1682303 days = 2 } }
	}

	#Refuse the request
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 60
			modifier = {
				JAP = { has_completed_focus = JAP_new_allied_member }
				factor = 0.75
			}
			modifier = {
				NKO = {
					OR = {
						NOT = { exists = yes }
						is_puppet_of = ROOT
						is_subject_of = ROOT
					}
				}
				factor = 0.5
			}
			modifier = {
				NKO = { exists = yes }
				factor = 0.1
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.1682302.oB
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.1682302.oB"
		set_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_NF_ANTICCP_KOR_SUPPORT_REFUSED
		JAP = { country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.1682310 days = 2 } }
	}
}

#North Korea Rejects the Alternative Guarantee

	id = mdmosjap_japan.1682316
	title = mdmosjap_japan.1682316.t
	desc = mdmosjap_japan.1682316.d
	#picture = GFX_news_event_hearts_of_iron_4

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = mdmosjap_japan.1682316.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.1682316.oA"
		add_political_power = -100
		if = {			# RoK didn't reject yet, propose to RoK
			limit = {
				KOR = { exists = yes }
				NOT = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_JAP_KOREAN_INTERVENTION_SOUTH_KOREA_REFUSED_GUARANTEE }
			}
			KOR = { country_event = mdmosjap_japan.1682322 }
			set_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_JAP_KOREAN_INTERVENTION_NORTH_KOREA_REFUSED_GUARANTEE
		} else = {		# RoK already rejected, end event cycle
			set_global_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_IMPENDING_JAPANESE_INTERVENTION_IN_KOREAS
		}
	}
}
