#Japan Accepts Our Demand
country_event = {
	id = mdmosjap_japan.1682342
	title = mdmosjap_japan.1682342.t
	desc = mdmosjap_japan.1682342.d
	#picture = GFX_news_event_hearts_of_iron_4

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	#Let's Sign the Agreement!
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 25
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.1682342.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.1682342.oA"
		add_stability = 0.03
		set_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_NF_ANTICCP_NKO_SUPPORT_ACCEPTED
		if = {
			limit = { JAP = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_NF_ANTICCP_NKO_SUPPORT_NEGOTIATION_SEARCH_FOR_ABDUCTEES } }
			set_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_NF_ANTICCP_NKO_ALLOWED_TO_SEARCH_FOR_ABDUCTEES
		}
		JAP = { country_event = mdmosjap_japan.1682314 }
		if = {
			limit = { JAP = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_NF_ANTICCP_NKO_SUPPORT_NEGOTIATION_1 } }
			NKO = { add_timed_idea = { idea = JAP_NKO_anticcp_NKOcompensation_1 days = 1825 } }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { JAP = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_NF_ANTICCP_NKO_SUPPORT_NEGOTIATION_2 } }
			NKO = { add_timed_idea = { idea = JAP_NKO_anticcp_NKOcompensation_2 days = 1825 } }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { JAP = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_NF_ANTICCP_NKO_SUPPORT_NEGOTIATION_3 } }
			NKO = { add_timed_idea = { idea = JAP_NKO_anticcp_NKOcompensation_3 days = 1825 } }
		}
	}

	#Demand More! They Should Accept Building the Nuclear Power Plant!
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 75
			modifier = {
				FROM = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_JAPNKO_PEACE_TREATY_ACCEPTED }
				factor = 0.04
			}
			modifier = {
				ROOT = {
					AND = {
						NOT = { has_country_leader = { name = "Kim Jong-il" } }
						NOT = { has_country_leader = { name = "Kim Jong-Un" } }
						NOT = { has_country_leader = { name = "Kim Jong-un" } }
						NOT = { has_country_leader = { name = "Kim Jong-chul" } }
						NOT = { has_country_leader = { name = "Kim Yo-jong" } }
					}
				}
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.1682342.oB
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.1682342.oB"
		JAP = { country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.1682343 days = 2 } }
	}
}

			limit = { JAP = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_NF_ANTICCP_NKO_SUPPORT_NEGOTIATION_SEARCH_FOR_ABDUCTEES } }
			set_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_NF_ANTICCP_NKO_ALLOWED_TO_SEARCH_FOR_ABDUCTEES
		}
		JAP = { country_event = mdmosjap_japan.1682314 }
		if = {
			limit = { JAP = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_NF_ANTICCP_NKO_SUPPORT_NEGOTIATION_1 } }
			NKO = { add_timed_idea = { idea = JAP_NKO_anticcp_NKOcompensation_1 days = 1825 } }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { JAP = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_NF_ANTICCP_NKO_SUPPORT_NEGOTIATION_2 } }
			NKO = { add_timed_idea = { idea = JAP_NKO_anticcp_NKOcompensation_2 days = 1825 } }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { JAP = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_NF_ANTICCP_NKO_SUPPORT_NEGOTIATION_3 } }
			NKO = { add_timed_idea = { idea = JAP_NKO_anticcp_NKOcompensation_3 days = 1825 } }
		}
	}

#First Choice (2000)
country_event = {
	id = Japan_Demographic.100001001
	title = Japan_Demographic.100001001.t
	desc = Japan_Demographic.100001001.d
	picture = GFX_JAP_diet_address

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	#Support for families
	option = {
		name = Japan_Demographic.100001001.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Japan_Demographic.100001001.oA"
		set_country_flag = JAP_DEMOGRAPHICS_CHAIN_APPEALED_CONSERVATIVES
		add_political_power = 50
		increase_social_spending = yes
		block_social_decrease = yes
		if = {
			limit = { has_socialist_government = yes }
			steal_popularity_from_conservatives = yes
		}
		else = {
			set_party_index_to_ruling_party = yes
			set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.03 }
			set_temp_variable = { temp_outlook_increase = 0.03 }
			add_relative_party_popularity = yes
		}

		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
		}
	}

	#Talk up workers' rights
	option = {
		name = Japan_Demographic.100001001.oB
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Japan_Demographic.100001001.oB"
		set_country_flag = JAP_DEMOGRAPHICS_CHAIN_APPEALED_PROGRESSIVES
		add_political_power = -50
		add_stability = -0.02
		if = {
			limit = { has_economically_liberal_government = yes }
			steal_popularity_from_progressives = yes
			set_temp_variable = { temp_opinion = -5 }
			change_small_medium_business_owners_opinion = yes
			change_industrial_conglomerates_opinion = yes
			change_international_bankers_opinion = yes
		}
		else = {
			set_party_index_to_ruling_party = yes
			set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.03 }
			set_temp_variable = { temp_outlook_increase = 0.03 }
			add_relative_party_popularity = yes
		}

		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
		}
	}
}

#Conservatives Demand More
country_event = {
	id = Japan_Demographic.100001002
	title = Japan_Demographic.100001002.t
	desc = Japan_Demographic.100001002.d
	picture = GFX_JAP_small_shop

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = JAP
		has_economically_liberal_government = yes
		has_country_flag = JAP_DEMOGRAPHICS_CHAIN_APPEALED_CONSERVATIVES
		NOT = {
			OR = {
				has_idea = fast_growth
				has_idea = economic_boom
			}
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 365
		modifier = {
			has_stability < 0.5
			factor = 0.2
		}
		modifier = { # if economy stays healthy, stay off player's back
			has_idea = fast_growth
			factor = 3
		}
		modifier = { # if economy stays healthy, stay off player's back
			has_idea = economic_boom
			factor = 5
		}
	}

	#Accept
	option = {
		name = Japan_Demographic.100001002.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Japan_Demographic.100001002.oA"
		set_temp_variable = { corp_change = -3 }
		modify_corporate_tax_rate_effect = yes
		set_temp_variable = { temp_opinion = 5 }
		change_small_medium_business_owners_opinion = yes
		change_industrial_conglomerates_opinion = yes
		change_international_bankers_opinion = yes

		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
		}
	}

	#Stuff it!
	option = {
		name = Japan_Demographic.100001002.oB
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Japan_Demographic.100001002.oB"
		add_political_power = -150
		set_temp_variable = { temp_opinion = -10 }
		change_small_medium_business_owners_opinion = yes
		change_industrial_conglomerates_opinion = yes
		change_international_bankers_opinion = yes
		set_party_index_to_ruling_party = yes
		set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = -0.01 }
		set_temp_variable = { temp_outlook_increase = -0.01 }
		add_relative_party_popularity = yes

		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
		}
	}
}

#Progressives Demand More
country_event = {
	id = Japan_Demographic.100001003
	title = Japan_Demographic.100001003.t
	desc = Japan_Demographic.100001003.d
	picture = GFX_JAP_labor_protest

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = JAP
		has_economically_liberal_government = yes
		has_country_flag = JAP_DEMOGRAPHICS_CHAIN_APPEALED_PROGRESSIVES
		NOT = {
			has_completed_focus = JAP_protect_worker_rights
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 365
		modifier = {
			has_stability < 0.5
			factor = 0.6
		}
	}

	#No way!
	option = {
		name = Japan_Demographic.100001003.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Japan_Demographic.100001003.oA"
		set_party_index_to_ruling_party = yes
		set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = -0.10 }
		set_temp_variable = { temp_outlook_increase = -0.10 }
		add_relative_party_popularity = yes
		set_country_flag = JAP_DEMOGRAPHICS_CHAIN_REFUSED_PROGRESSIVES

		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
		}
	}

	#Accept union interests
	option = {
		name = Japan_Demographic.100001003.oB
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Japan_Demographic.100001003.oB"
		add_political_power = -300
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = industrial_conglomerates
			}
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = industrial_conglomerates
				add_idea = labour_unions
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { party_index = 0 }
		set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.03 }
		add_relative_party_popularity = yes
		set_temp_variable = { party_index = 7 }
		set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.02 }
		set_temp_variable = { temp_outlook_increase = 0.02 }
		add_relative_party_popularity = yes
		set_temp_variable = { party_index = 15 }
		set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.02 }
		set_temp_variable = { temp_outlook_increase = 0.02 }
		add_relative_party_popularity = yes
		set_temp_variable = { party_index = 20 }
		set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.03 }
		set_temp_variable = { temp_outlook_increase = 0.03 }
		add_relative_party_popularity = yes
		set_temp_variable = { party_index = 21 }
		set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.03 }
		set_temp_variable = { temp_outlook_increase = 0.03 }
		add_relative_party_popularity = yes

		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
		}
	}
}

#First Depopulation Checkup Gate (2002)
#This is more gentle in consequences than the main sequence checkups
country_event = {
	id = Japan_Demographic.100003200
	hidden = yes

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Japan_Demographic.100003200.oA"
		if = { #You blew it!!
			limit = {
				check_variable = { jap_demographics_depopulation_reform < 1 }
			}
			JAP = { country_event = Japan_Demographic.100003201 }
		} else_if = { #Problems ahead!
			limit = {
				check_variable = { jap_demographics_depopulation_reform < 2 }
			}
			JAP = { country_event = Japan_Demographic.100003202 }
		} else = { #Doing great!
			JAP = { country_event = Japan_Demographic.100003203 }
		}
	}
}

		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Japan_Demographic.100003203.oA"
		add_political_power = 50
		set_party_index_to_ruling_party = yes
		set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.05 }
		set_temp_variable = { temp_outlook_increase = 0.05 }
		add_relative_party_popularity = yes
		activate_mission = JAP_demographic_main_reminder

		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
		}
	}

	#Extend our program!
	option = {
		name = Japan_Demographic.100003203.oB
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Japan_Demographic.100003203.oB"
		increase_social_spending = yes
		set_temp_variable = { corp_change = 2 }
		modify_corporate_tax_rate_effect = yes
		set_temp_variable = { pop_change = 2 }
		modify_population_tax_rate_effect = yes
		if = { #only if eco conservative
			limit = { has_economically_liberal_government = yes }
			steal_popularity_from_progressives = yes
		}
		else = {
			set_party_index_to_ruling_party = yes
			set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.03 }
			set_temp_variable = { temp_outlook_increase = 0.03 }
			add_relative_party_popularity = yes
		}
		activate_mission = JAP_demographic_main_reminder

		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
		}
	}

	#Amend the budget
	option = {
		name = Japan_Demographic.100003203.oC
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Japan_Demographic.100003203.oC"
		add_political_power = 100
		set_temp_variable = { corp_change = -3 }
		modify_corporate_tax_rate_effect = yes
		set_temp_variable = { treasury_change = 50 }
		modify_treasury_effect = yes
		if = { #only if not already conservative
			limit = { has_socialist_government = yes }
			steal_popularity_from_conservatives = yes
		}
		else = {
			set_party_index_to_ruling_party = yes
			set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.03 }
			set_temp_variable = { temp_outlook_increase = 0.03 }
			add_relative_party_popularity = yes
		}
		activate_mission = JAP_demographic_main_reminder

		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
		}
	}
}

#Replace Industrial Conglomerates with Labor Union?
country_event = {
	id = Japan.100001001
	title = Japan.100001001.t
	desc = Japan.100001001.d
	picture = GFX_JAP_labor_protest

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = JAP
		has_idea = industrial_conglomerates
		NOT = {
			has_idea = labour_unions
		}
	}

	#Better not
	option = {
		name = Japan.100001001.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Japan.100001001.oA"
		add_political_power = 100

		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
		}
	}

	#Accept union interests
	option = {
		name = Japan.100001001.oB
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Japan.100001001.oB"
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = industrial_conglomerates
			}
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = industrial_conglomerates
				add_idea = labour_unions
			}
		}
		add_political_power = -200
		set_temp_variable = { temp_opinion = 10 }
		change_labour_unions_opinion = yes
		set_temp_variable = { party_index = 0 }
		set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.01 }
		add_relative_party_popularity = yes
		set_temp_variable = { party_index = 7 }
		set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.01 }
		set_temp_variable = { temp_outlook_increase = 0.01 }
		add_relative_party_popularity = yes
		set_temp_variable = { party_index = 15 }
		set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.01 }
		set_temp_variable = { temp_outlook_increase = 0.01 }
		add_relative_party_popularity = yes
		set_temp_variable = { party_index = 20 }
		set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.01 }
		set_temp_variable = { temp_outlook_increase = 0.01 }
		add_relative_party_popularity = yes
		set_temp_variable = { party_index = 21 }
		set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.01 }
		set_temp_variable = { temp_outlook_increase = 0.01 }
		add_relative_party_popularity = yes

		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
		}
	}
}


# Samurai Bonds Chain
country_event = {
	id = Japan.100002000
	title = Japan.100002000.t
	desc = Japan.100002000.d
	picture = GFX_JAP_yen

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #accept deal
		name = Japan.100002000.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: Japan.100002000.oA executed"
		set_temp_variable = { treasury_change = 30 }
		modify_treasury_effect = yes
		FROM = {
			country_event = Japan.100002001
		}
		set_temp_variable = { percent_change = 0.5 }
		set_temp_variable = { tag_index = FROM.id }
		set_temp_variable = { influence_target = ROOT.id }
		change_influence_percentage = yes
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = FROM
			modifier = economic_mission
		}
		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = FROM
			modifier = economic_mission
		}

		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				has_opinion = {
					target = FROM
					value < -50
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #refuse deal
		name = Japan.100002000.oB
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: Japan.100002000.oB executed"
		FROM = {
			country_event = Japan.100002002
		}

		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_opinion = {
					target = FROM
					value > 30
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

	desc = Japan.100004010.d

	is_triggered_only = yes

	# Accept deal
	option = {
		name = Japan.100004010.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: Japan.100004010.oA executed"
		add_tech_bonus = {
			name = Japan.100004010.t
			bonus = 1
			uses = 1
			category = internet_tech
		}
		set_temp_variable = { percent_change = 0.5 }
		set_temp_variable = { tag_index = FROM.id }
		set_temp_variable = { influence_target = ROOT.id }
		change_influence_percentage = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					OR = { #only care to get a receipt from global if a major power or larger accepts
						has_idea = superpower
						has_idea = great_power
						has_idea = large_power
					}
					OR = { #if SEA, we want to know and potentially offer investments
						is_SE_Asia = yes
					}
				}
			}
			FROM = {
				country_event = Japan.100004011
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				has_opinion = {
					target = FROM
					value < -50
				}
			}
		}
	}
	# Refuse deal
	option = {
		name = Japan.100004010.oB
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: Japan.100004010.oB executed"
		add_political_power = 25

		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				has_opinion = {
					target = FROM
					value > 30
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# Contribution to IHPCO
country_event = {
	id = Japan.100004141
	title = Japan.100004141.t
	desc = Japan.100004141.d
	picture = GFX_JAP_anchor_generic

	is_triggered_only = yes

	# Accept
	option = {
		name = Japan.100004141.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: Japan.100004141.oA executed"
		add_to_variable = {
			var = JAP.jap_ihcpo_funding_amt
			value = 1
		}
		FROM = { country_event = Japan.100004142 }
		set_temp_variable = { treasury_change = -10 }
		modify_treasury_effect = yes
		add_to_array = { FROM.jap_ihpco_members = ROOT.id }

		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				has_opinion = {
					target = FROM
					value < -50
				}
			}
		}
	}
	# Refuse
	option = {
		name = Japan.100004141.oB
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: Japan.100004141.oB executed"
		add_political_power = 25
		FROM = { country_event = Japan.100004143 }

		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_opinion = {
					target = FROM
					value > 30
				}
			}
		}
	}
	# More Funding
	option = {
		name = Japan.100004141.oC
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: Japan.100004141.oC executed"
		add_to_variable = {
			var = JAP.jap_ihcpo_funding_amt
			value = 2
		}
		add_political_power = -50
		set_temp_variable = { treasury_change = -30 }
		modify_treasury_effect = yes
		add_to_array = { FROM.jap_ihpco_members = ROOT.id }
		FROM = { country_event = Japan.100004142 }

		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				has_opinion = {
					target = FROM
					value > 30
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_opinion = {
					target = FROM
					value < -50
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# Supercomputing Results Gate
country_event = {
	id = Japan.100004144
	hidden = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Japan.100004144.oA"
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { jap_ihcpo_funding_amt < 5 }
			}
			for_each_scope_loop = {
				array = JAP.jap_ihpco_members
				country_event = { id = Japan.100004145 } # Supercomputing Bad Outcome
			}
		} else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { jap_ihcpo_funding_amt < 8 }
			}
			for_each_scope_loop = {
				array = JAP.jap_ihpco_members
				country_event = { id = Japan.100004146 } # Supercomputing Good Outcome
			}
		} else = {
			for_each_scope_loop = {
				array = JAP.jap_ihpco_members
				country_event = { id = Japan.100004147 } # Supercomputing Amazing Outcome
			}
		}
	}
}

#[KATO] Start of Kato Rebellion Scenario
#Gate, when triggered chooses between an event or nothing, and sets one of two flags either way
country_event = {
	id = mdmosjap_EDT.120412001
	hidden = yes

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				JAP = {
					OR = {
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 0 }
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 1 }
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 7 }
					}
				}
			}
			JAP = {
				country_event = mdmosjap_japan_kato.1
				set_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_KATO_REBELLION_EXECUTED
			}
		} else = {
			JAP = { set_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_KATO_REBELLION_AVERTED }
		}
	}
}

			has_country_leader = { name = "Kim Jong-il" }
		}
		JAP = {

		}
	}

	option = {
		NKO = { country_event = mdmosjap_japan.131222001 }
		JAP = { country_event = mdmosjap_japan.131222002 }
	}
}

		}

country_event = {
    id = japan_foreign_policy.6
    title = "japan_foreign_policy.6.title"
    desc = "japan_foreign_policy.6.desc"
    picture = "GFX_report_event_trade_conference"

    is_triggered_only = yes # This event is triggered by specific conditions or actions.

    option = { # Option A: Create or Expand FTAAP
        name = "japan_foreign_policy.6.option.a"
        ai_chance = { factor = 50 }

        # Conditions based on government type
        if = {
            limit = { NOT = { government = liberal } }
            add_political_power = -200
            add_popularity = { ideology = radical_right amount = 0.08 }
            add_popularity = { ideology = radical_left amount = 0.04 }
        }

        # Notify CHI and TAI about FTAAP entry
        CHI = { country_event = { id = japan_foreign_policy.7 days = 2 } }
		# Enter FTAAP?(CHI)
        TAI = { country_event = { id = japan_foreign_policy.8 days = 2 } }
		# Enter FTAAP?(TAI)
    }

    option = { # Option B: Better not
        name = "japan_foreign_policy.6.option.b"
        ai_chance = { factor = 50 }

        # Apply effects if not a liberal government
        if = {
            limit = { NOT = { government = liberal } }
            add_political_power = 150
            add_party_popularity = { ideology = current_government_ideology amount = 0.03 }
        }

        # Conditional event trigger for Japan's reaction
        if = {
            limit = { 
                NOT = { has_completed_focus = FTAAP_focus }
                NOT = { has_country_flag = took_ftaap_route }
            }
            # Trigger an event reflecting Japan's stance against globalization
            JAP = { country_event = { id = japan_foreign_policy.9 days = 2 } }
        }
    }
}

    is_triggered_only = yes 
	# Triggered by Japan's FTAAP actions

        name = "japan_foreign_policy.7.option.a"
        tooltip = "Joining the FTAAP will bolster our economic growth, provided Taiwan Province is not invited by Japan."
        
        # Conditional action based on the status of Taiwan's invitation
        if = {
            limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = taiwan_invited_to_ftaap } }
            add_political_power = -100
            add_ideas = china_ftaap_engagement_idea

            # Modify opinions based on FTAAP support without Taiwan's invitation.
            JAP = { add_opinion_modifier = { target = THIS modifier = ftaap_supportive } }
        }
        else = {
            add_political_power = 50
            tooltip = "Japan has invited Taiwan authorities, complicating our decision to join."
        }
    }

    option = { # Option B: Refuse to join FTAAP because Taiwan authorities are being invited
        name = "japan_foreign_policy.7.option.b"

        add_political_power = 150
        add_ideas = china_ftaap_refusal_idea

        JAP = { add_opinion_modifier = { target = THIS modifier = ftaap_refusal } }

        name = "japan_foreign_policy.7.option.c"

            limit = { has_country_flag = taiwan_invited_to_ftaap }
            add_opinion_modifier = { target = TAI modifier = ftaap_china_inclusive }
        }
    }

        tooltip = "Given the current geopolitical tensions and pressures, it's in our best interest to not join the FTAAP."

        # Effects of Taiwan deciding against joining the FTAAP.
        add_political_power = 100
        add_stability = 0.05
    }

    option = { # Option A: Create or Expand FTAAP, insist on primacy
        name = "japan_foreign_policy.12.option.a"
        tooltip = "We will push forward with the FTAAP, asserting our leadership role while managing our relationship with the USA."
        
        add_political_power = 100
        add_popularity = { ideology = radical_right amount = 0.02 }
        add_popularity = { ideology = radical_left amount = 0.02 }
        # Applying a relations penalty with the USA as a consequence of insisting on primacy
        USA = { add_opinion_modifier = { target = THIS modifier = ftaap_tension } }
        USA = { country_event = { id = usa_ftaap_decision.1 days = 2 } }
    }

    option = { # Option B: Create or Expand FTAAP, accept USA's primacy
        name = "japan_foreign_policy.12.option.b"
        tooltip = "Acknowledging the USA's primacy can facilitate the FTAAP's creation, ensuring smoother international cooperation."
        
        add_popularity = { ideology = radical_right amount = 0.05 }
        add_popularity = { ideology = radical_left amount = 0.02 }
        # Triggering an event for the USA to potentially take credit for the FTAAP
        USA = { country_event = { id = usa_ftaap_credit.1 days = 2 } }
    }

    option = { # Option C: Better not proceed with FTAAP
        name = "japan_foreign_policy.12.option.c"
        tooltip = "The potential drawbacks at this juncture outweigh the benefits of pursuing the FTAAP further."
        
        if = {
            limit = { NOT = { government = liberal } }
            add_party_popularity = { ideology = current_government_ideology amount = 0.03 }
        }
        add_political_power = 50
        # Conditional trigger for a significant event if FTAAP has not been pursued and focuses are complete
        if = {
            limit = { 
                NOT = { has_completed_focus = FTAAP_focus }
                NOT = { has_country_flag = took_ftaap_route }
            }
            JAP = { country_event = { id = japan_foreign_policy.11 days = 2 } }
        }
    }

#Japan Turns Against Globalization!

    desc = "japan_foreign_policy.11.desc"
    picture = "GFX_report_event_japanese_nationalism"

    is_triggered_only = yes # This event is triggered by specific conditions reflecting Japan's stance on globalization.

    option = { # Option A: Japan First!
        name = "japan_foreign_policy.11.option.a"
        tooltip = "Prioritizing our domestic economy and small businesses, we adopt a 'Japan First' stance towards globalization."
        
        # Effects on domestic sectors and political landscape
        add_opinion_modifier = {
            target = small_businesses
            modifier = small_business_boost
            opinion = 20
        }
        add_opinion_modifier = {
            target = conglomerates
            modifier = conglomerate_skepticism
            opinion = -10
        }
        add_opinion_modifier = {
            target = international_bankers
            modifier = international_banker_skepticism
            opinion = -10
        }
        add_party_popularity = { ideology = right_wing_populism amount = 0.10 }
    }

    option = { # Option B: Fair, Not Free Trade
        name = "japan_foreign_policy.11.option.b"
        tooltip = "We advocate for fair trade practices that benefit all, rather than unchecked free trade."
        
        add_political_power = 100
        add_party_popularity = { ideology = non_aligned_communism amount = 0.10 }
        set_country_flag = japan_fair_trade_focus
    }

        	JAP = {
            	add_political_power = 500
        	}
    	}
        
        CHI = { 
            add_political_power = 50 
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = JAP
				modifier = minor_improve_trade
			}
            # TODO: Sets flag to give additional bonuses for completing “East Asian Community”
        }
		TAI = {
			add_political_power = -50
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = JAP
				modifier = minor_deteriorate_trade
			}
		}
    }

    option = { # Option B: Support Taiwan's Independence
        name = "japan_foreign_policy.14.option.b"
        tooltip = "Supporting Taiwan's independence stance strengthens our ties with Taipei but risks our relationship with Beijing."
        EVENT
        add_political_power = 50
        # Applying diplomatic and trade penalties with China
		
        CHI = {  
            add_political_power = -50
			add_opinion_modifier = { 
				target = JAP 
				modifier = minor_deteriorate_trade 
			}
        }
        TAI = { 
            add_political_power = 100
			add_opinion_modifier = { 
				target = CHI 
				modifier = minor_improve_trade 
			}
            # TODO: Sets flag for TAI to weigh towards rejecting unification and ultimatums from CHI
        }
    }

    option = { # Option C: Encourage a Permanent Agreement
        name = "japan_foreign_policy.14.option.c"
        tooltip = "Encouraging a permanent agreement between China and Taiwan could pave the way for lasting peace and stability in the region."
        
        add_political_power = -100
        CHI = { 
            add_political_power = 100 
            # TODO: Sets flag for CHI to weigh towards Two China focus
        }

            add_stability = 0.05 
        }
    }
}

			}
            JAP = {
                create_faction = "East Asian Alliance"
                add_to_faction = CHI
            }
        }
        else = {
            limit = { 
				CHI = { 
					is_in_faction = yes 
				} 
			}
            JAP = { 
				join_faction = CHI 
			}
        }
        USA = { 
			country_event = { 
				id = japan_foreign_policy.262 
				days = 2 
			} 
		}
    }
}
